Ụlọ akwụkwọ ndị nnwere onwe nke Scotland wepụtara onwe ha na iwete gburugburu mmụta ga-akwadobe ụmụaka ma jiri nka ndị achọrọ wee kwadobe ha iji mee nke ọma, ihe ọ bụla ọdịnihu wetere.
Enweghị ike ịgọnarị ya n’oge a, na gburugburu azụmahịa ụwa, na asụsụ gara n’ihu na adị oke mkpa n’ọdịnihu nke obodo, yabụ ekwesịrị igosipụta nke a n’agụmakwụkwọ.
N’ezie, ekwesịrị ịhụta asụsụ ọhụụ ka “nka nkwukọrịta ofesi.”
Ụlọ akwụkwọ ndị nnwere onwe ga-aga n’ihu na enye nhọrọ a, ndịiche na ọkachamma maka ndị ntorobịa nke Scotland.
Il faut bien le faire.
John Edward bụ Onye Nduzi nke Nzụkọ nke Ụlọ Akwụkwọ Ndị Nnwere Onwe nke Scotland
Lebron ga-apụta izizi maka ndị Lakers na Sọnde na San Diego
Ọchịche abịabele na njedebe maka ndị nsuso na eche ịhụ LeBron James mee mbido izizi ya maka Los Angeles Lakers.
Onye ndu ndị Lakers Luke Walton ekwuola na James ga-eso n’egwuregwu nke nkwadobe afọ asọmpi na Sọnde n’etiti Denver Nuggets na San Diego.
Mana nkeji ole ọ ga-egwu egwuregwu ka amatabeghị.
“Ọ ga-akarị otu mana ọ gaghị eru 48,” nke Walton kwuru na weebụsaịtị ndị Lakers ziri ezi.
Onye mkpesa akụkọ nke Lakers Mike Trudell dere na James nwere ike igwu obere egwuregwu.
Isochi nkwadobe na mbido nke izu a, ajụrụ James maka atụmatụ ya maka usoro nke nkwadobe afọ asọmpi egwuregwu isii nke Lakers.
“Achọghị m egwuregwu a na-eme n’oge mmalite n’ọnọdụ m ugbu a n’ọrụ m, iji dị nkwadebe,” o kwuru.
Oge nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ Trump nke West Virginia. Youtube Channel
Onye Isi Ala Donald Trump malitere ọtụtụ nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ ọchịchị na Wheeling, West Virginia.
Ọ bụ nke izizi n’ime nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ ise achịkọbara Trump n’izu ise na-abịa, tinyere ebe nkwụsị nke ndị enyi tinyere Tennessee na Mississippi.
N’ijigide ntuli aka nkwado onye nhọrọ nke ya ịbanye n’ọkwa Ụlọ Ikpe Kachasị Elu ghe oghe,Trump na-atụ anya ịkwalite nkwado maka ntuli aka ọkara ọchịchị na-abịa, ebe ndị otu Repọblikan nọ n’ihe egwu nnarapụ njikwa Ụlọ Ọmebe iwu mgbe a ga-atụnye aka na Nov.
Kedu oge bụ nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ West Virginia nke Trump n’abalị a, yana kedu ka ị ga-esi lelee ya n’ịntanetị.
Etinyere nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ Trump nke Wheeling West Virginia na elekere 7 nke abalị. ET, Satọde, Septemba 29, 2018.
I nwere ike lelee nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ Trump nke West Virginia n’ịntanetị, n’okpuru site na ihe nkiri ozugbo na Youtube.
Trump nwere ike ikwu maka nnụrịta ụka nke izu a banyere onye nhọpụta Ụlọ Ikpe Kachasị Elu Brett Kavanaugh, nke malitere ịdị ọgbaghara n’ihi ebubo ihe mmekọrịta nwoke na nwanyị yana ntuli aka nkwado Nzụkọ Ọmeiwu a na-atụ anya ya ejigidere ihe ruru otu izu mgbe ndị FBI na-eme nyocha.
Mana isi atụmatụ ọtụtụ nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ a bụ inyere ndị otu Repọblikan aka na ntuli aka Nọvemba siri ike nwetakwa agbamume.
Ya mere, ndọrọndọrọ ọchịchị Onye Isi Ala Trump kwuru na nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ nke izu ise a na-abịa bụ maka “ịgba ndị na-enyere aka akwụ ụgwọ na ndị nkwado ume, ka ndị otu Repọblikan na-agbalị ichekwa ma gbasaa na ịmịrịkịtị ha ji na Nzụkọ Ọmeiwu Iwu nke Nnukwu na nke Obere” dabere na ndị Reuter.
“Njikwa Ụlọ Ọmebe Iwu dị oke mkpa maka atụmatụ ya, nke na onye isi ala ga-eje ọtụtụ obodo ka ọ nwere ike, ka anyị na-abanye n’oge ndọrọndọrọ ọchịchị” onye nkwuchite okwu ndọrọndọrọ ọchịchị Trump nke achọghị ka akpọ aha ya gwara Reuters.
Etinyere na Ama Wesbanco Wheeling, nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ abalị a nwekere ike ịkpọta ndị nkwado si “Ohio na Pennsylvania ma dọrọ mkpuchi site na mgbasa ozi Pittsburgh,”dabere na West Virginia Metro News.
Satọde ga-abụ ugboro nke abụọ n’ọnwa gara aga Trump gara West Virginia, obodo nke o meriri site na ihe karịrị akara pesentị 40 na 2016.
Trump na-agbali ịnyere onye ahọpụtara maka Nzụkọ Ọmeiwu Repọblikan West Virginia Patrick Morrisey aka, bụ onye nke na-akpụ akpụ na nyocha.
“Ọ bụghị ezigbo akara dịịrị Morrisey na onye isi ala ga-abịa iji kwalite ya na nyocha,” Simon Haeder kwuru, onye nyocha sayensị ndọrọndọrọ ọchịchị na West Virginia University, dabere na Reuters.
Ryder Cup 2018: Ndị otu USA gosiri afọ ịlụ ọgụ iji dobe olile anya were banye na asompi agba nke otu onye na Sọnde
Ka akụchara agba otu akụkụ ugboro atọ, agba mmadụ anọ nke ehihe Satọde nwere ike bụrụ ihe Ryder Cup a chọrọ.
Ike nke nkuli ihe bụ kpamkpam atụmatụ egwuregwu achọpụtara mana ọ bụ nke ndị na-egwu egwuregwu kwenyere na ya, nke pụtakarịrị ihie na ụdị asompi dị otu a.
Yabụ kedu ebe ha ga-ekwu na ike dị ugbu a?
“Ha ji akara isii aga ma ugbu a ọ bụ anọ, yabụ anyị ga-ebu nke ahụ dịka obere agbamume, a na m eche,” Jordan Spieth kwuru ka ọ na-apụ maka ụbọchị ahụ.
Mba Europe nwere uru, n’ezie, akara anọ n’ihu yana iri na abụọ a ka na-akụ akụ.
Ndị America, dịka Spieth kwuru, chere na ha nwere obere ikuku n’ubu ha ma nwee ọtụtụ ihe agbamume, na abụghị opekempe ụdịdị Spieth na Justin Thomas, bụ ndị gwukọrọ egwuregwu ọnụ ụbọchị niile, na onye ọ bụla ga-anya isi akara atọ n’ime anọ.
Spieth dị mmerụ ahụ kemgbe akụpụrụ na tee ruo na ama ndu ndu ma na-aga dịka ọmụmatụ.
Mkpu ike nke anurị dasibere ike ka agba nke ya na-aga n’ihu, n’ịkụbanye bọọlụ dị mkpa iji mee ka egwuregwu nke anọ nọrọ n’otu akara mgbe ya na Thomas jiri ọkụkụ abụọ ‘na-akpụ akpụ ka ha kụchara ugboro abụọ.
Ụdị olu mkpu ahụ zutere ya na nkụbanye nke nyere ha mmeri na 15, ụdị nke na-agwa gị na ọ kwenyere na ndị America apụbeghị na nke a.
“Ị ga-enyobanye anya n’ime were na-atụ uche maka egwuregwu nke gị,” Spieth kwuru.
Ọ bụ naanị ihe ndị niile na-akụ egwuregwu a nwere ugbu a.
Oghere18 iji nwee akara.
Naanị ndị na-akụ egwuregwu a nwere akara karịa Spieth na Thomas n’ime ụbọchị abụọ gara aga bụ Francesco Molinari na Tommy Fleetwood, akụkọ nke Ryder Cup enweghị mgbagha.
Njikọ mara mma ma na atụghị anya nke Europe bụ anọ n’ime anọ n’enweghị ike ime ihe ọjọọ ọ bụla.
“Moliwood” bụ naanị njikọ na-akụfeghị na ehihe Satọde, mana ha zenarịrị nkụfe n’ụtụtụ Satọde, ehihe Fraịde yana ngwucha oghere itoolu n’ụtụtụ Fraịde.
Ọkụkụ ahụ, na ka ike ha si aga ma na-abịa site na ndị igwe mmadụ a na-eme mkpọtụ gosipụtara na ha bụ ndị egwuregwu a ga-achọ imeri na Sọnde, nke n’agaghị enwe onye egwuregwu ọzọ ama ama nwere ike bute mmeri nke mba Europe ka anwụ na-ada na Le Golf National karịa Fleetwood na Molinari.
Ọ kacha mma ha abụọ n’otu oge n’oghere dị iche iche.
Okwu ebube mba Europe erubeghị, agbanyeghi.
Bubba Watson na Webb Simpson jiri Sergio Garcia mere ihe egwuregwu na bọọlụ otu mmadụ abụọ n’ụtụtụ, mgbe etinyekọrọ yana Alex Noren.
Ịkụfe otu ugboro na ịkụfe ugboro abụọ n’ọkụkụ ugboro itoolu kụnyere onye mba Spain na Sweden n’olulu nke ha enweghị ike ịrịpụta.
Na Sọnde, agbanyeghị n’onweghị onye ga-enyere gị aka ịpụta n’olulu gị.
Bọọlụ otu mmadụ abụọ na agba mmadụ anọ bụ ihe ịtụ n’anya ịnọ nso lelee n’ihi mkparịta ụka dị na etiti njikọ a, ndụmọdụ ha na-enye, ndụmọdụ ha anaghị enye na otu atụmatụ na-esi agbanwe ozugbo ozugbo.
Mba Europe akụọla nke ọma dịka otu ruo ugbu a ma werekwa isi pụtara ihie ruo n’ụbọchị ikpeazụ mana agba mmadụ anọ a gosiri na otu USA nwere afọ ilụ ọgụ nke na ụfọdụ, ọ kachasị ndị Stateside na-agbagha mgbagha.
Mba Europe ji 10-6 aga, were banye Ryder Cup n’ụbọchị ikpeazụ
Mba Europe ga-eji uru mara abụba were banye ụbọchị ikpeazụ nke Ryder Cup ka ha jichara 10-6 aga United State na bọọlụ otu mmadụ abụọ yana agba mmadụ anọ nke Satọde.
Ndị abụọ a akpalitere mmụọ ha, Tommy Fleetwood na Francesco Molinari bu ụzọ site na mmeri abụọ emeriri Tiger Woods n’agbalị mgbalị, n’iji akara anọ aga na Le Golf National.
Ndị otu mba Europe nke Thomas Bjorn, na-achụ ijigide iko mmeri anapụrụ ha na Hazeline afọ abụọ gara aga, nọgidere ndị mba America na-akụgheri akụgheri ike na bọọlụ otu mmadụ abụọ n’ụtụtụ, were 3-1 merie agba nke ahụ.
Ndị US zọgidere nke ukwuu na agba mmadụ anọ, wee merie na asompi abụọ, mana ha enweghị ike ibelata ọnụọgụ mmeri.
Otu Jim Furyk chọrọ akara asatọ site na asompi 12 agba nke otu onye mere na Sọnde iji jigide iko mmeri ha.
Fleetwood bụ onye ọhụrụ mbụ mba Europe meriri akara anọ ugboro ugboro ebe ya na Molinari, agụrụ aha “Molliwood” ka izu ụka pụrụ iche gachara bụ otu abụọ jiri akara anọ merie na asompi izizi anọ ha na hịstrị Ryder Cup.
Ebe ha merigoro Woods na Patrick Reed na bọọlụ otu mmadụ abụọ, ha were jikọọ nke ọma were merie Woods dagoro mba na onye ọhụrụ mba America, Bryson Dechambeau site na 5&4 dara ụda.
Woods, bụ onye dọgidere onwe ya na asompi abụọ na Satọde gosiri anya nka ya na adanye adanye mana o tufuola asompi 19 n’ime 29 na bọọlụ otu mmadụ abụọ yana agba mmadụ anọ na nke asaa ugboro ugboro.
Justin Rose zuru ike bọọlụ otu mmadụ abụọ nke ụtụtụ, were laghachi isonyere Henrik Stenson na agba mmadụ anọ nke ejiri 2&1 were merie Dustin Johnson na Brooks Koepka-ndị nọ n’ọkwa nke mbu na nke atọ na mba ụwa.
Mba Europe enwetachaghị ya ka ha siri chọọ, agbanyeghị n’ụbọchị ikuku ọma mgbada ọdịda anyanwu nke Paris.
Jordan Spieth onye mmeri ugboro atọ na Justin Thomas jiri akara abụọ were tọọ ọkọlọtọ maka mba America na Satọde.
Ha nwetara mmeri siri ike nke 2&1 na Jon Rahm na Ian Poulter nke mba Spain na bọọlụ otu mmadụ abụọ were laghachi ọzọ imeri Poulter na Rory Mcllroy 4&3 na agba mmadụ anọ, ebe emerigoro ha n’oghere mmalite abụọ.
Naanị ugboro abụọ na hịstrị Ryder Cup ka otu laghachiri azụ site na akara anọ ejiri emeri ha na mbanye agba nke otu onye, n’agbanyeghị dịka ndị ji iko, otu Furyk chọrọ naanị ịgbata onye laba, onye laba iji jigide iko mmeri ha.
Mgbe ha gbachara ndị nke abụọ n’ụbọchị abụọ, kosiladị, mbuso agha nke Sọnde dị ka ihe karịrị ha.
North Korea kwuru “ọ gaghị eme” ịgbarapụ ngwa ọgụ na anataghị nkwenye
Onye Mịnịsta nke mba ofesi North Korea gwara United Nations na Satọde na ịga n’ihu amachibido ha na-ebute atụkwasịghị obi na United State nke na ọ nweghịkwa ka obodo ha ga-esi gbarapụ ngwa ọgụ nuklịa ha n’ụdị ọnọdụ ahụ.
Ri Yong Ho gwara otu mba ụwa na Mgbakọ Ezumezu ha kwa afọ na North Korea esorola “ezigbo ụzọ pụtara ihie” n’afọ gara aga, dị ka nkwụsị nlele ngwa nuklịa na ogbunigwe, ntọsa ebe nlele ngwa nuklịa ma kwee nkwa na ọ gaghị arụkasị ngwa ọgụ nuklịa na teknụzụ nuklịa.
“Kosiladị, anyị ahụghị asịsa na-esote ya sitere na U,S” o kwuru.
“N’enweghị ntụkwasị obi na U.S, agaghị enwekwa okwukwe na nchekwa nke obodo anyị, na n’ụdị ọnọdụ a, ọ nweghị ka anyị ga-esi buru ụzọ gbarapụ ngwa ọgụ anyị.”
Ebe Ri gbanwere mkpesa ndị North Korea banyere ọjụjụ nke Washington ime usoro “agba” mgbarapụ ngwa nuklịa n’okpuru nke North Korea ga-erite elele dịka ọ na-esonye usoro obere obere, okwu ya bara uru n’ihi na ọ jụghị mgbarapụ ngwa nuklliya ozugbo dịka Pyongyang siri mee n’oge gara aga.
Ri rụtụrụ aka na nkwuputa Kim Jong Un na Donald Trump kwukọrịtara na ọgbakọ nke izizi n’etiti onye isi ala U.S nọ n’ọchịchị na onye ọchịchị North Korea na Singapore na Juun 12, mgbe Kim kwere nkwa ịhụ banyere “mgbarapụ ngwa nuklịa nke okirikiri Korea” ebe Trump kwere nkwa nchekwa nke North Korea.
North Korea na-achọ njedebe agha 1950-53 nke Korea, mana United States ekwuola na Pyongyang ga-ebu ụzọ gbarapụ ngwa ọgụ nuklliya ya.
Washington ajụkwala oku ibelata mmachibido mba ụwa a siri ike nke North Korea.
“U.S kwụgidere na “mgbarapụ ngwa nuklịa-izizi” ma bulikwuo nkwanye ya site na mmachibido iji mezuo ebumnuche ha n’ụzọ nkwanye, ma jụkwuo “nkwuputa nke njedebe agha” Ri kwuru.
“Nghọta na mmachibido ga-akputu anyị n’ikpere anyị bụ nrọ efu nke ndị na amaghị anyị.
Mana nsogbu bụ na ịganihu eme machibido na-emina enweghị ntụkwasị obi anyị.”
Ri ekwughị maka atụmatụ ọgbakọ nke abụọ n’etiti Kim na Trump nke onye ọchịchị U.S kwuturu na United Nation n’izu ahụ.
Kama mịnịsta ahụ kwuturu maka nzụkọ atọ n’etiti Kim na onye ọchịchị South Korea Moon Jae-in n’ime ọnwa ise gara aga were tinyekwa: “Ọ bụrụ na ndị ọ metutara n’okwu nke mgbarapụ ngwa nuklịa bụ South Korea na ọ bụghị U.S, mgbarapụ ngwa nuklịa nke okirikiri Korea agaghị abịa n’ụdị nkụchikọ a.”
Ọbụlagodi otu a, olu okwu Ri tụgharịrị nke ukwuu site na afọ gara aga, mgbe ọ gwara Mgbakọ Ezumezu U.N. kwuru na iji rọketị ndị North Korea wee nweta isi ala U.S. apụghị ime, ka “Ajọ Onye Isi Ala” Trump kpọrọ Kim “nwoke rọketị” nọ n’ọrụ igbu ọchụ.
N’afọ a na United Nations, Trump onye nke majara n’afọ gara aga “imebi kpam kpam” North Korea, kpokwasara Kim otito maka obi ọ nwere n’isoro usoro mgbarapụ ngwa agha, mana o kwuru na a ka nwere ọtụtụ ọrụ nke na mmachibido ka ga-adịgide ruo mgbe North Korea kwụsịrị ngwa nuklịa.
Na Wenesde, Trump kwuru na ọ nweghị oge ewepụtara maka nke a, na-ekwu “ọ bụrụ na ọ ga-ewe afọ abụọ, afọ atọ ma ọ bụ ọnwa ise- ọ nweghị ihe ọ pụtara.”
China na Russia na-arụrịta ụka na Ọgbakọ Nchekwa U.N. kwesịrị inye Pyongyang elele maka usoro ndị ha megoro.
Kosiladị, U.S Mike Pompeo gwara Ọgbakọ Nchekwa U,N Na Tọsde na “Mmanye nke mmachibido Ọgbakọ Nchekwa ga-aga n’ihu ike n’ike na-adaghị mba ruo mgbe anyị mezuru mgbarapụ ngwa nuklịa kpam kpam, na njedebe.”
Ọgbakọ Nchekwa ahụ jikọrọ aka ọnụ kwalite mmachibido North Korea kemgbe 2006, n’ụzọ ịgbachi ego maka mmemme ngwa nuklịa na ogbunigwe Pyongyang.
Pompeo zutere Ri n’akụkụ nke Mgbakọ Ezumezu U.N. wee gwa ya ka emechara na ọ ga-abịa Pyongyang ọzọ n’ọnwa na-abịa iji kwado maka ọgbakọ nke abụọ.
Pompeo ejeela North Korea ugboro atọ n’afọ a, mana njem ikpeazụ ya agaghị nke ọma.
Ọ hapụrụ Pyongyang na Julaị na-ekwu na enwela agamnihu, naanị ka North Korea jụ ya n’ime awa ole ma ole maka iti “iwu yiri nke ndị agboro.”
North Korea kwere nkwa na nzụkọ yana Moon mere n’ime ọnwa a ịtọsa ebe ogbunigwe nakwa ụlọ ọrụ nuklịa ma ọ bụrụ na United States esoro “usoro dabara.”
O kwuru na Kim gwara ya, “usoro dabara” nke ọ na-achọ bụ nkwa nchekwa Trump kwere ya na nkwa na Singapore yana ịga n’ihu mee ka mmekọrịta dị n’etiti Washington dị mma.
Ụmụ akwụkwọ Harvard na-eme mmụta ka-esi enwe ezumike zuru ezu
Mmụta ọ hụrụ dị na Mahadum Harvard n’afọ a mere ụmụ akwụkwọ niile na-agụ akwụkwọ ịrahụzu ụra, ime ka echere omenala iji kafin agụ akwụkwọ ‘abalị niile’ aka mgba.’
Onye mmụta chọpụtara na ụmụ akwụkwọ enwere na Mahadum mbu n’ụwa niile anaghị amakarị ihe kwesịrị ma abịa n’ilekọta onwe ha anya.
Charles Czeisler, ọkammụta ahụike nke ụra na Havard Medical School yana onye ọkachamara na Brigham yana Women Hospital haziri mmụta ahụ, nke ọ kwenyere na ọ bụ ụdịdị ya mbu na US.
Ọ nwetara echiche ịmalite mmụta ahụ ka ọ nyechara nkuzi banyere nsonazụ arahụghị ụra na-eme mmụta.
‘Ka emechara nke ahụ otu nwa agbọghọ biakwutere m nwee sị: ‘Kedu ihe kpatara o jiri bụrụ ugbu a ka a na-agwa m ihe a, n’afọ senịọ m?’
O kwuru na ọ nwebeghị onye gwara ya uru ụra bara- bụ ihe tụrụ m n’anya.’ ọ gwara The Telegraph.
Nkuzi ahụ, nke ebupụtara n’izizi ya n’afọ a, kọwaara ụmụ akwụkwọ ka uru akparamagwa ezigbo ụra si enyere agumakwụkwọ yana ime mmemme egwuregwu aka, ma dozikwaa ahụ ha niile.
Paul Barreira, ọkammụta ọrịa ọgụgụ isi na mmụọ na Harvard Medical School yana onye isi oche ọrụ ahụike nke mahadum, kwuru na mahadum ahụ kpebiri ịmalite mmụta ahụ ka achọpụtara na ụmụ akwụkwọ anaghị arahụzu ụra n’ime izu.
Mmụta ahụ ruru otu awa tinyere usoro ọrụ mkparịta ụka.
N’otu ngalaba enwere onyonyo ime ụlọ ụra, ebe ụmụ akwụkwọ na-apịdo n’iko kọfị, akwa mgbochi, akpụkpụ ụkwụ egwuregwu yana akwụkwọ iji gwa ha banyere nsonazụ kafin na ihie yana ka arahụghị ụra siri emetụta mmemme egwuregwu, n’uru mmemme oge ụra dị.
Na ngalaba ọzọ, agwara ndị sonyere ka arahụghị ụra ogologo oge siri akpalite ihe egwu obi nkolopu, mkpọnwu ahụ, mmụọ ịda mba yana oria mkpụrụ akụ.
Maapu ụlọ akwụkwọ nwere akara ngosi mkparịta ụka, wee na-akwado ndị sonyere ka ha chee banyere ihe ha na-eme kwa ụbọchị.
‘Anyị maara na ọ gaghị agbanwe agwa ụmụ akwụkwọ ozugbo.
Mana anyị kwenyere na ha nwere ikike ịmata- dịka inwere ikike ịmata nsonazụ nhọrọ ise siga n’ahụike,’ Ọkammụta Czeisler gbakwunyere.
Omenala ngala ‘ịmụ anya abalị niile’ ka dịkwa, o kwuru, tinyere teknụzụ agbara ọhụrụ yana mbawanye nkwanye na-adakwasa ụmụ akwụkwọ, pụtara na arahụghị ụra bụ nsogbu n’ebuwaye.
Ịgba mbọ hụ na inwetara ụra zuru ezu, dị mma, kwesịrị ịbụ ngwa agha nwata akwụkwọ’ iji chere mgbakasị ahụ, ike ọgwụgwụ na obi mmapụ aka mgba, o kwuru - ọbụlagodi izenari ntinye ahụ, ka arahụghị ụra na-etinye ụbụrụ n’ọnọdụ oke agụụ, na-eme ha agụụ kwa mgbe.
Raymond So, nwata gbara afọ 19 nke California na-agụ kemikal na fisikal baịyọlọji nyere Ọkammụta Czeisler aka ịhazi mmụta ahụ, ebe o megoro otu klaasị ya n’afọ gara aga n’ime oge afọ izizi ya na Harvard.
O kwuru na mmụta ahụ mepere anya ya wee kpalite echiche ya ịkwanye ka mmụta a bụrụ maka ụlọ akwụkwọ niile.
Nke na-esote ya, ọ na-enwe olile anya ịrịọ ụmụ akwụkwọ ndị gụchagoro mmụta izizi ka ha mejuputa mmụta yitebere nke a tupu ha abanye n’ụlọ akwụkwọ ahụ.
Ọkammụta Czeisler kwadoro ka ụmụ akwụkwọ chee banyere itinye otimkpu maka mgbe ha chọrọ ịrahụ ụra, yana mgbe ha chọrọ ikuli, ma marakwa maka nsonazụ mmerụ ahụ ihuenyo ngwa eletrọnịk “ihie agba elu igwe” na-ebute yana ihie LED, nke nwere ike kụpụ usoro ka ahụ gị si akpa agwa, we bute nsogbu ịrahụ ụra.
Livingston 1-0 Rangers: Goolu Menga buturu ndị nke Gerrard
Rangers natara ihe mgbu ka ọgbụgba Dolly Menga kwanyere akụkụ Steven Gerrard ghasara aghasa na mmeri 1-0 emeriri ha na Livingston.
Akụkụ Ibrox ahụ na-achọ inweta mmeri nke izizi ha n’ụzọ kemgbe ha meriri 4-1 na Febuarị na St Johnstone, mana ndị otu Gary Holt nyere Gerrard mmeri nke abụọ emeriri ha n’egwuregwu 18 dịka onye njikwa jiri akara asatọ esegharị n’elu nke ndị mbu na Ladbrokes Premiership, Hearts.
Menga jiri tupu nkeji asaa nke ọkara oge were gbanye ọkpụ, na ndị Rangers n’enweghị mkpalite mmụọ adịghị ka ndị ga-agbanyekwa nke ha.
Ebe ndị Rangers gbadara na ndị nke isii, Linvingston gbagoro na ndị nke atọ ma jiri ndịiche dị na goolu nọrọ naanị n’azụ Hibernian.
Na enwere ike inwe nsogbu n’ọdịnihu maka ndị Rangers ka agwọchara onye na-akwụ n’akụkụ Calum Spencem merụ ahụ n’isi, mgbe atụchara ihe si n’akụkụ nke ndị ọbịa.
Gerrard mere mgbanwe asatọ n’akụkụ nke gbafere Ayr were banye n’agba na-esote nke ikpeazụ nke Iko Betfred.
Holt, n’aka nke ya, jiri otu 11 Livi wee gaa, nke napụrụ ndị Hearts otu akara izu gara aga, na ọ gaara ịmasịkwa ya otu ndị nke ya gbasiri ike siri sogide ndị iro ha n’ebe niile.
Rangers nwere ike bụrụ ndị kacha jide bọọlụ mana Livingston kacha jiri bọọlụ ha nwetere wee mere ihe.
Ha kwesịrị iji nkeji abụọ ha jiri banye nye goolu mgbe obere ọkpụkpa izizi nke Menga mere zipuru Scott Pittman na goolu nke Allan McGrego, mana onye nke ahụ na-agba n’etiti gbafuru nnukwu oghere ya.
Ọgbụgba Keaghan Jacobs mere zutere onye na-eche goolu Craig Halkett mana onye mgbachibido otu ya Alan Lithgow nwere naanị ike ịgbafu ya n’azụ.
Rangers nwetara njikwa mana ọ dịka enwere olile anya karịa ka enwere nkwenye ka otu ha si agba na ngwucha nke atọ.
Alfredo Morelos chere na ọ kwesịrị ịgba penaliti n’akara nkeji iri na ise ka ya na Steven Lawless kụtara mana onye njikwa egwuregwu Steven Thomson lefere mkpesa onye Columbia ahụ anya.
Rangers gbalịrị naanị ịgbata na postu ugboro abụọ n’ọkara nke mbu mana onye na-echeburu ndị Ibrox goolu Liam Kelly enweghị ihe mmekpa ahụ ọ bụla na nke Lassana Coulibaly jiri isi kụọ yana ọgbụgba adaghị ụda Ovie Ejaria gbara.
Ebe goolu nkeji 34th ndị Livi gbara nwere ike bụrụ ndapụta, ọ nweghị onye ga-ekwu na ọ dabarọ ha naanị maka mbọ ha gbara.
Ọzọkwa Rangers enweghị ike metụta ọkpụkpa Jacob miri emi.
Scott Arfield enweghị ihe ọ mere ka Declan Gallagher gbanyere Scott Robinson bọọlụ, bụ onye dara juu were họrọ Menga maka ịgbachapụ ya.
Gerrard megharịrị na oge ezumike dị ka o jiri Ryan Kent gbanwee Coulibaly nke metụrụ mmetụta ozugbo, ka onye nke na-agba n’akụkụ fanyere Morelos mana Kelly na-agba nke ọma gbara ọsọ site na ebe ọ nọ bịa gbochie.
Mana Livingston gara n’ihu ime ka ndị ọbịa ahụ na-agba ụdị egwuregwu na-amasị ha, ebe Lithgow na Halkett na-agba bọọlụ ote aka kwa mgbe.
Akụkụ Holt kaara ịgbatị mmeri ha n’oge ikpeazụ mana McGregor kwuchiri wee jụ Jacobs, tupu Lithgow ewere isi kụpụ bọọlụ n’akụkụ.
Onye nnọchite nke Rangers Glenn Middleton nwere mkpesa maka penaliti nke abịaghị n’oge ka ya na Jacobs kụkọrọ mana Thomson lefere anya ọzọkwa.
Almanak: Onye mepụtara ngụ Geiger
N’Ugbu a otu ibe sitere na Almanak “Ụtụtụ Sọnde” anyị: Septemba 30, 1882, afọ136 gara aga taa, wee Na-agụ ... ụbọchị nke amụrụ onye nke ga-abụ onye fiziks n’ọdịnihu Johannes Wilhem “Hans” na Germany.
Geiger mepụtara ụzọ esi achọpụta ma lelee nha redioaktiviti, nchọpụta nke mechara bute ngwa a na-akpọ Ngụ Geiger.
Ebe ndabere sayensi kemgbe, Ngụ Geiger mechara bụrụkwa ndabere agbụrụ ọhụrụ, dịka n’ihe nkiri 1950 “Bells of Coronado.” ndị nọ na ya adịchaghị ka ndị nyocha sayensi na-achị ehi Roy Rogers na Dale Evans:
Nwoke: “Ọ gịnị n’elu ụwa nke a bụ ihe ahụ?”
Rogers: “Ọ bụ ihe Ngụ Geiger, ejiri achọpụta ebe ihe nnweta dị n’ala nọ dịka uranium.
Mgbe ịgbanwuru ngwa nti a, i nwere ike ịnụ nsonazụ atọm na-enye sitere na redioaktiviti dị na ihe nnweta dị n’ala.”
Evans: “Kwuo, ọ na-eme eme ugbu a!”
“Hans” Geiger nwụrụ n’afọ 1945, naanị mkpụrụ ụbọchị ole ma ole ruo ụbọchị ọmụmụ 63 ya.
Mana nchọpụta nke bu aha ya dịịrị gaba.
Ọgwụ mgbochi ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ ọhụrụ nwere ike ikuziri sistem nchekwa ahụ ka ọ “hụ” selụ na-emebi ihe
Ọgwụ mgbochi ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ ọhụrụ nwere ike ikuziri sistem nchekwa ahụ ka ọ “hụ” selụ na-emebi ihe ma gbuo ha
Ọgwụ mgbochi na-akuziri sistem nchekwa ahụ ka ọ mata selụ na-emebi ihe dịka ụzọ ọgwụgwọ ọrịa
Ụzọ a tinyere ịmịpụta selụ nchekwa ahụ n’ahụ onye ọrịa, were gbanwee ya n’ụlọ nyocha
Ha nwere ike ‘ịhụ’ protin na-adịkarị n’ọtụtụ ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ, were gbaghachi ya azụ
Ọgwụ mgbochi eji eme nlele na-egosi ndapụta nyere afọ ojuju na ndị ọrịa nwere ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ dị iche iche.
Otu nwanyị ejiri ọgwụ mgbochi ahụ were gwọ, nke na-akuziri sistem nchekwa ahụ ịmata selụ na-emebi ihe, hụrụ ka ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ nke akpa akwa ya pụrụ ihe karịrị ọnwa 18.
Ụzọ ahụ tinyere ịmịpụta selụ nchekwa ahụ n’ahụ onye ọrịa, were gbanwee ya n’ụlọ nyocha ka ha were ‘hụ’ protin na-adịkarị n’ọtụtụ ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ a na-akpọ HER2, wee gbaghachi selụ ndị ahụ azụ.
Ọkammụta Jay Berzofsky nke US National Cancer Institute dị na Bethesda Maryland, kwuru: “Ndapụta anyị na-egosi na anyị nwere ọgwụ mgbochi nyere afọ ojuju.”
HER2 ”na-akwa uto nke ọtụtụ ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ,” tinyere ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ nke ara, akpa akwa, ngu na ọwa nsi, Ọkammụta Berzofsky kọwara.
Usoro yitebere inwepụ selụ nchekwa ahụ n’ahụ onye ọrịa were “kuziere” ha ka-esi achọpụta selụ ọrịa mkpụrụ akụ arụọla ọrụ n’ịgwọ otu ụdị ọrịa ụmị ọkpụkpụ.
Kanye West Gara Njem Okwu Iwe Binyere Trump, Yiri Okpu MAGA, Ka Ọ Pụtachara na SNL.
Ọ Gaghị Nke Ọma
Etikporo Kanye West mkpu n’ụlọ egwu ahụ n’oge Saturday Night Live ka ọ mechara ihe nkiri ọ na-atagheri ọnụ nke otoro Onye Isi Ala Donald Trump nke U.S. were kwuo na ọ ga-apụta zọọ ọkwa na 2020.
Ka ọ gụchara egwu nke atọ ya n’abalị ahụ, akpọrọ Ghost Town nke oyi okpu Make America Great, ọ gara n’ihu ikwutọ ndị Demokrat were kwuputakwa nkwado ya maka Trump.
“Ọtụtụ oge m na onye ọcha kparịtara ụka, ha ekwuo: “Kedu ka isi nwee mmasị na Trump, ọ bụ onye kpọrọ onye isi ojii asị?”
N’ezie, ọ bụrụ na omume ịkpọ onye isi ojii asị na-emetụta m, agaara m apụ na America kemgbe.” o kwuru.
SNL jiri obere ihe ịkpa ọchị wee malite ihe nkiri ahụ nwere Matt Damon, ebe onye ama ama nke Hollywood ahụ mere akaja nkwuputa Brett Kavanaugh n’ihu Ọgbakọ Ndị Ikpe nke Nzụkọ Ọmeiwu maka ebubo mwakpo nwanyị Christine Blasey Ford boro ya.
N’agbanyeghị na agbasaghị ya n’ikuku, onye mkpa ọchị Chris Rock bugoro ihe nkiri okwu iwe West ahụ na ụzọ mgbasa ozi mmekọrịta ọha.
O doghị anya ma Rock ọ chọrọ ime West akaja site na mbusa ozi ahụ.
Ọzọkwa, West kpesara ndị n’elele ihe nkiri ahụ na emechuru ya ihu n’azụ ụlọ banyere okpu isi ya.
“Ha gwara okwu m ọjọọ n’azụ ụlọ.
Ha sịrị, ‘eyikwala okpu ahụ were pụọ ebe ahụ.’
Ha gwara m okwu ọjọọ!
Ha wee kwukwa ọzọ, na m nọ n’ime ebe omimi.” o kwuru, dabere na Washington Examiner.
West gara n’ihu. “Ị chọrọ ịhụ ebe ihe omimi ahụ?” na-ekwu na ya ga-eyibe uwe superman ya, nke pụtara na ịgaghị agwa m ihe m ga-eme. Ị chọrọ ka ụwa gaa n’ihu?
Nwalee ịhụnanya.”
Okwu ya kpalitere mkpu site na ndị n’elele ihe nkiri ahụ opekempe ugboro abụọ na ndị ọrụ SNL mere ka ndị emechuru ihu, Variety na-ekwu, nke otu onye na-agwa akwụkwọ ozi ahụ: “Ụlọ egwu ahụ niile dara juu.”
Ewebatara West dịka onye nnọchi anya onye ọgụ egwu Ariana Grande n’oge ikpeazụ, bụ onye nke enyi ya nwoke na mbu, na-akụ egwu rap Mac Miller nwụrụ na mkpụrụ ụbọchị ole ma ole gara aga.
West tinyere ọtụtụ mmadụ na mgbagwoju anya n’iyi uwe dịka Kalama Perrier were kụọ egwu I Love it ahụ.
West nwetara nkwado site na onye isi otu TPUSA, Candace Turner, bụ onye nke dere na twitter: “Maka otu n’ime ndị nwere mmụọ siri ike: DAALỤ MAKA ỊKWỤGIDE N’IHU NDỊ IGWE MMADỤ.”
Mana onye nchịkọba ihe nkiri okwu Karen Hunter dere na twitter na West naanị “bụ onye ọ bụ, na nke a bụ ihe mara oke mma.”
“Mana A họrọ m na m “AGAGHỊ” enye mmadụ elele (site na ịzụ egwu ya ma ọ bụ uwe ya ma ọ bụ kwado “nka” ya} bụ Onye nke m kwenyere na ọ na-amakọ ma na-ekwuputa nkwenye dị mmerụ ahụ n’obodo.
Ọ nwegoro onwe ya.
Yabụ ma anyị onwe anyị,” ọ gbakwunyere.
Tupu ihe nkiri ahụ onye ọkụ egwu rap a, kwuputara na Twitter na ya agbanwego aha ya,na-ekwu na ọ bụ “onye nke amaara na mbu ka Kanye West.”
Ọ bụghị onye na-eme ihe egwuregwu izizi nke gbanwere aha ya, na-esonye na nzọ ụkwụ Diddy, onye amakwara ka Puff Daddy, Puffy na P.Diddy.
Onye ọkụ egwu rap ibe ya, Snoop Dogg enwela mgbe ọ zara Snoop Lion, ọzọkwa onye ọkụ egwu bụ ọkaibe Prince, gbanwere aha ya ka ọ bụrụ akara yana onye na-eme ihe egwuregwu amaburu dịka Prince.
Ịgba akwụkwọ maka ịnwa igbu ọchụ n’ihi ịsụ mma n’ụlọ oriri na ọṅụṅụ Belfast.
Agbaala otu nwoke dị afọ 45 akwụkwọ maka ịnwa igbu ọchụ, ka asụchara otu nwoke mma n’ụlọ oriri na ọṅụṅụ dị na ọwụwa anyanwụ Belfast na Fraịde.
Ihe mmereme ahụ mere na Ballyhackamore, onye uwe ojii kwuru.
A tụrụ anya na onye ahụ nke na-agọrọ onwe ya ga-abịa n’obere ụlọ ikpe Belfast na Mọnde.

Onye na-eme ihe nkiri Game of Thrones Kit Harrington akụsuola n’ihi ọrụ dịrị nwoke dị njọ
Ejiri ịpịa mma mara Kit Harrington dịka Jon Snow na ihe nkiri HBO Game of Thrones nwere ihe egwu nke dabere na echiche agba ochie.
Mana nwoke ahụ na-eme ihe nkiri a, 31, akụsuola ejirimara enwere maka ndị dike, na-ekwu na ụdị ime ejije a n’ihuenyo pụtara na ụmụaka ndị nwoke ga-eche na ha kwesịrị isi ike tupu ha enweta nsọpụrụ.
Mgbe ọ na-agwa The Sunday Times Culture, Kit kwuru na ọ kwenyere ‘n’ihe emebiela’ wee jụọ ka a ga-esi were luso nsogbu ọrụ dịrị nwoke dị njọ ọgụ n’oge #MeToo.
Kit, onye nke lụrụ onye ya na ya na-emekọ ihe nkiri Game of Thrones Rose Leslie, dịkwa 31, kwetara na ọ ‘na-emetụta ya nke ukwuu’ banyere ịkpatụ aka n’okwu ahụ.
‘N’onwe m, ọ na-emetụta m nke ukwuu, ugbu a - kedu ebe anyị gabigara n’ọrụ dịrị nwoke?,’ o kwuru.
‘Kedu ihe anyị na-akuziri ụmụ-nwoke mgbe ha na-etolite etolite, n’ihe banyere nsogbu anyị na-ahụ ugbu a?’
Kit kwenyere na igwe ihe nkiri ketere obere oke maka mbawanye ọrụ dịrị nwoke dị njọ, ekele dịịrị agwa ụmụ-nwoke n’ihe nkiri.
Ọ gara n’ihu: ‘Kedu ihe bụ ọnatarachi na nke akuziri akuzi?
Kedu ihe a na-akuzi n’igwe ihe nkiri, yana n’ime ogbe na-eme ka ụmụaka ndị nwoke chee na ha kwesịrị ịdị ụdị akụkụ a na nwoke?
A na m eche na nke ahụ bụ nnukwu ajụjụ n’oge anyị a -kedu ka anyị ga-esi gbanwee ya?
N’ihi o doro anya na ọ nwela ihe mebiri n’ụmụaka ndị nwoke anyị.’
N’ajụjụ ọnụ ahụ ọ kwetara na ya agaghị eme akụkọ mmalite ma ọ bụ nke nsochi Game of Thrones ma ejije ahụ bịa na njedebe n’oge okpomọkụ na-abịa, na-ekwu na ya na ama ịlụ agha na ịnyịnya emechela’.
Site na na Novemba Kit ga-apụta na mmegharị Sam Shepard True West nke bụ akụkọ maka onye na-emepụta ihe nkiri na nwanne ya nwoke, bụ onye ohi.
Nwoke ahụ na-eme ihe nkiri kwuputara n’oge adịghị anya na ọ na-eche na izute nwunye ya Rose bụ ihe kachasị mma mere ya na Game of Thrones.
‘Ezutere m nwunye m n’ihe nkiri a, yabụ n’ụzọ nke ahụ o nyere m ezinụlọ m n’ọdịnihu, ya na ndụ m were dịrị gaba.’ o kwuru.
Rose mere Ygritte, bụ onye Kit na eṅomi, Jon Snow hụrụ n’anya, n’ejije nwetara awọdụ Emmy.
Di na nwunye ahụ lụrụ na Juun 2018 n’ala ogige be Leslie na Scotland.
HIV/Ọrịa obiri n’aja ọcha: China n’akọ na-enwere mgbali 14% n’okwu ọhụrụ
China mara ọkwa na-enwere mgbali 14% n’ọnụọgụ ndị amaala ya nwere HIV na Ọrịa obiri n’aja ọcha.
Ihe karịrị mmadụ 820,000 ka ọ metụtara n’obodo ahụ, ndị ọrụ ahụike na-ekwu.
Ihe ruru okwu 40,000 ọhụrụ ka ekpesara naanị n’ime agba nke abụọ na nkeji anọ 2018.
Ọtụtụ n’ime okwu ọhụrụ a bụ site na n’ụzọ mmekọrịta nwoke na nwanyị ka esiri bufee ya, na-egosi mgbanwe n’oge gara aga.
N’omenala, HIV gbasara ngwangwa n’akụkụ ụfọdụ China n’ihi ọbara ndị butere ọrịa agbanyere ha.
Mana ọnụọgụ ndị na-ebute HIV n’ụzọ a, ebelatala ihe ruru efu, ndị ọrụ ahụike China kwuru n’ọgbakọ emere n’okirikiri Yunnan.
Afọ n’elu afọ, kosiladị, ọnụọgụ ndị nwere HIV na Ọrịa obiri n’aja ọcha ejirila mmadụ 100,000 gbalie.
Nbufe HIV site na mmekọrịta nwoke na nwanyị bụ okwu siri ike n’ogbe LGBT ndị China.
Ewepuru ịda iwu dị n’okwu mmekọrịta nwoke na nwoke ma ọ bụ nwanyị na nwaanyị na China na 1997, mana mkpachapụ ndị LGBT ka dị nnukwu.
N’ihi ụkpụrụ nchekwa nke obodo ahụ, mmụta nyocha na-ama amụma n’ihe ruru 70-90% ụmụ nwoke ndị na-enwe mmekọrịta nwoke na nwoke ga-emecha lụọ nwanyị.
Ọtụtụ n’ime mbufe ọrịa ndị ahụ na esite na-emeghị mkpuchi mmekọrịta nwoke na nwanyị zuru oke n’ime ịme enyi ndị a.
Kemgbe 2003, gọọmentị China ekwela nkwa nweta ọgwụ HIV bụ ozurumba dịka mbọ ha imegide okwu ahụ.
Maxine Waters agọla agụgọ na onye ọrụ ya bụ onye busara data ndị ọmebe iwu GOP, kwutọọ ‘asị ọjọọ’ na ‘amụma ịkpa nkata’
U.S. Onye ọmebe iwu Maxine Waters na Satọde gọnarịrị ebubo na otu onye ọrụ ya tinyere ozi nkeonwe nke ndị ọmebe iwu atọ Repọblikan U.S. na ibe ọmebe iwu Wikipedia.
Onye Los Angeles Demokrat ahụ kwusiri ike na ndị na-ebusa ebubo ahụ bụ ndị otu “ultra-right wing” na ndị websaịtị.
“Asị, asị, na asị ọjọọ,” Waters kwuru na nkwuputa na Twitter.
Ozi nke ahụ ewepụtara nwere adreesị ụlọ na akara ekwentị maka Ndị Ọmebe Iwu U.S Lindsey Graham nke South Carolina, na Mike Lee yana Orrin Hatch, ha abụọ bụ ndị Utah.
Ozi ahụ pụtara n’ịntanetị na Tọsde, nke amaghị onye tinyere ya na Capitol Hill n’oge nnụrịta ụka ọgbakọ Nzụkọ Ọmeiwu banyere ebubo mmekọrịta nwoke na nwanyị eboro onye nhọpụta Ụlọ Ikpe Kachasị Elu Brett Kavanaugh.
Mbusa ahụ pụtara mgbe ndị ọmebe iwu mmadụ atọ gbara Kavanaugh ajụjụ.
Ndị saịtị nchekwa ụkpụrụ dịka Gateway Pundit na Redstate kwuputara na adreesị IP ejiri mara ebe ozi ahụ siri busa metụtara ụlọ ọrụ Waters, wee wepụta ozi nke onye ọrụ Waters, Hill kwuputara.
“Ebubo a n’enwegh isi bụ ụgha kpamkpam yana asị zuru ezu,”Waters gara n’ihu.
“Onye ọrụ m nke emebigoro nzuzo onye ọ bụ, ozi nkeonwe na nchekwa ya n’ihi ebubo aghụghọ na ụgha ndị a - enweghị ka aka ya siri dị na mbusa ozi ahụ.
Ebubo a n’enweghị isi bụ ụgha kpamkpam yana asị zuru ezu.”
Nkwuputa Waters kpalitere nkọcha ozugbo n’ịntanetị, tinyere onye n’ahụ maka mgbasa ozi White House gara aga Ari Fleischer.
“Ngọnarị a dị iwe,” Fleischer dere.
“Nke a pụtara na ọ nweghị ụdị mmụọ eji a bụ Onye Ọmebe Iwu.
Mgbe eboro mmadụ ihe ha emeghị, ha ekwesịghị iwe iwe.
Ha ekwesịghị ịrụ ụka.
Ha ekwesịghị ịjụ ebumnuche onye boro ebubo.
Ha kwesịrị ịdị nwayọọ ma daa jụụ.”
Ọ bịara dịka Fleischer na-atule omume Waters na nkọcha ndị Demokrat mere Ọka Ikpe Kavanaugh, bụ onye nke ndị nkọcha boro ebubo na ọ dịka ọ were nnukwu iwe n’oge nnụrịta ụka Tọsde.
Omar Navarro, bụ onye nke Repọblikan na-achọ ịnapụ Waters oche n’oge ntuli aka ọkara ọchịchị, kwuputakwara echiche ya na Twitter.
“Nnukwu ma ọ bụrụ eziokwu,” ọ dere.
Na nkwuputa ya, Waters kwuru na ụlọ ọrụ ya akpọturugo “ ndị ikike dị n’aka na ndị mmanye iwu banyere ebubo ụgha ndị a.
“Anyị ga-ahụ na ndị mere ya ga-apụta ihie,” ọ gara n’ihu “na iwu ga-ejide ha maka omume ha niile nke na-emerụ ahụ ma dị egwu ebe onye na ndị ọrụ m niile nọ.
Nyocha Johnny English Strikes Again - buturu ihe nkiri nzuzo ịkpa ọchị Rowan Atkinson
Ọ bụ omenala ugbu a ịchọ mkpa Brexit n’ihe nkiri ọhụrụ ọ bụla nwere nribama Britain, na nke a dịka ọ metụtara mmegharị ihe nkiri ịkpa ọchị nke Johnny English - bụ nke ejiri Johnny English malite na 2003, wee laghachikwa azụ na 2011 ka Johnny English Reborn.
Ọ pụtara na ihe nkiri njakịrị nke isiokwu otu anyị siri bụrụ ndị iberibe pụtara ihie, bụzi oghere nbufe ahịa ọhụrụ anyị?
Kosiladị, onye nzuzu anya ọkpụ, ihu rọba Johnny English emegharịala ikike ya ịkwalite ihe nke ugboro abụọ - aha ya karịa ihe ọ bụla na-egosi na ọ bụ nchepụta ihe ịkpa ọchị emebere maka akụkụ obodo ndị anaghị asụ Bekee.
N’ezie ọ bụ onye iberibe ọrụ nzuzo nke agbanyeghị ṅṅomi ya gbagwojuru anya, nwere obere Clouseau, ntakịrị Mr Bean na nfechalụ nke nwoke ahụ n’etinye otu olu na isiokwu Chariots of Fire na mmalite mmemme Olympics London 2012.
N’izizi ọ dabere n’onye njem yana nwoke nzuzo mba ụwa Atkinson nke emere na ihe mgbasa ozi Barclaycard TV echefugoro, na-ahapu ọgbaghara n’azụ ya.
Enwere otu oge ma ọ bụ abụọ mara mma na JE ọhụrụ a.
Ọ masịrị m ka Johnny English na-erute nso n’ụgbọ elu ebe oyi uwe agha ndị agba ochie, igwe nkucha were na-akụta n’okpu agha ya.
Onyinye Atkinson nwere maka ịkpa ọchị a na-ahụ anya pụtara ihie, mana ịkpa ọchị ahụ esighi ike ma mafee oke, tụmadị ihe nkiri ndị ahụ “anaghị akpa ọchị” dịka 007 na Mission Impossible n’onwe ha na-enwekwa ihe ịkpa ọchị n’ime ya ugbu a.
Ihe ịkpa ọchị ahụ dịka ọ bụ ụmụaka ka emebere ya karịa ndị okenye, maka mụ onwe m njegheri Johnny English enweghị ihe nchepụta pụrụ iche yana ebumnuche ya dịka ihe nkiri anaghị ekwu okwu nke Atkinson, n’onye nke Bean.
Ebe mgbado ukwu isiokwu ugbu a bụ na Great Britain nọ n’oke nsogbu.
Onye nbanye ịntanetị anataghị ikike banyere na netwọk ndị ọrụ nzuzo kachasị dị nzuzo nke Britain, kpughee ndị ọrụ nzuzo niile nọ n’ọrụ, na mgbagwoju anya onye ọrụ nzuzo nọ ọrụ - obere ihe omume maka Kelvin Eldon.
Ọ bụ nke ikpeazụ maka onye isi ala bụ onye mpako nwere nsogbu, nke enweghịzi nkwado ọchịchị ọ bụla kpamkpam: Emma Thompson nwara ike ya na ime ihe omume a yitebere Teresa-May mana enwekebeghị ihe dị n’akwụkwọ ọ ga-eji rụọ ọrụ.
Ndị na-enye ya ndụmọdụ nchekwa gwara ya na ebe amagoro ndị ọrụ nzuzo ya niile, ọ ga-akpọpụta onye lagoro ezumike nka.
Nke ahụ pụtara Johnny English na-emegheri emegheri n’onwe ya, onye nke ewere n’ọrụ dịka onye nkuzi n’ụlọ akwụkwọ ndị ọgaranya, mana na-enye nkuzi nke adịghị n’akwụkwọ ka-esi a bụ onye ọrụ nzuzo: ọmalịcha odide ebe a, dịka English nyere ụdị ụlọ akwụkwọ nzuzo School of Rock.
Ebughachiri English na Whitehall maka inye ntuziaka ntụmadị were zukọta yana onye nke abụọ ya tagbugoro onwe ya n’ahụhụ Bough, bụ Ben Miller mere ya ọzọ.
Bough abụrụla onye lụrụ nwunye, ejikọrọ ya na onye isi ngwa ọgụ mmiri, bụ ihe omume onye nwere agba Vicki Pepperdine mere ka onye mmanya na-egbu.
Yabụ na Batman na Robin nke na emebi ihe mgbe niile N’ọrụ Nzuzo Her Majesty amalitekwala, na-ezute Olga Kurylenko dịka ọmalicha Ophelia Bulletova.
Kosiladị, onye isi ala na-adanye na anwansi nke onye ọgaranya tech, bụ onye nke kwuru na ọ nwere ike idozi nsogbu kọmputa ndị Britain nwere: onye ọjọọ Jason Volta bụ Jake Lacy mere ya.
English na Bough malitere njem nke egwuregwu nzuzu ịkpa ọchị ha: gbanwee dịka onye na-eke nri, ha mụnyere ọkụ n’ụlọ oriri na ọṅụṅụ French; ha butere ọgbaghara izunye onwe ha n’ime ụgbọ mmiri ezumike Volta; English kpalitere mgbagwoju anya ka ọ nwara iji ngwa isi Virtual Reality nwere mata ime ụlọ Volta.
Eji ihe niile were mee agba nke ikpeazụ ahụ, ma obi uto na egwumegwu niile dị ya, enwere obere TV ụmụaka dị n’ihe niile ahụ.
Ọmalịcha ihe agafeghị oke.
Dịka n’ihe nkiri Johnny English ndị ọzọ, ọ naghaghị m ịche: ndị na-eme ihe nkiri nke Britain enweghi ike nye Rowan Atkinson ihe omume ga-ebuputa onyinye ya nke ọma?
Labour na-agọnarị na ha anaghị akpa nkata atụmatụ ka ndị Britain na-arụ ọrụ ụbọchị anọ n’izu ma nara ụgwọ ọrụ maka ụbọchị ise
Labour Party nke Jeremy Corbyn na-atule atụmatụ ga-agbanwe ihe nke ga-ahụ na ndị Britain rụọ ọrụ ụbọchị anọ n’izu ha anara ụgwọ ọrụ maka ụbọchị ise.
Ndị otu a chọrọ ka ndị isi nwe ụlọ ọrụ na-enyefe akụ ha chekwabara n’aka ndị ọrụ siterena mgbanwe artificial intelligence (AI) site na inye ha ụbọchị ụma agaghị arụ ọrụ.
Ọ ga-eme na ndị na-arụ ọrụ ga-erite elele ụbọchị atọ n’izu ụka ma welakwaa otu ụgwọ ọnwa.
Ndị nzuputa okwu kwuru na echiche a “ga-adaba” na ebumnuche yana atụmatụ akụnụba nke otu a ime ka ọ dabaara ndị ọrụ.
Ndị otu Trades Union Congress akwadola ịmalite ụbọchị anọ n’ime izu dịka ụzọ ndị ọrụ ga-esi rite elele na akụnụba na-agbanwe.
Onye senịọ nzuputa okwu nke Labour Party gwara Sunday Times: ‘A na-atu anya ịma ọkwa nyocha amụma tupu ngwucha afọ a.
‘Ọ gaghị eme ozugbo mana ịrụ ọrụ ụbọchị anọ n’izu bụ ebumnobi ndị otu a dabara n’usoro ihazi akụnụba ka ọ dabaara ndị ọrụ yana mkpokota ụzọ nrụpụta ihe nke ndị otu ahụ.’
Labour Party agaghị abụ ndị izizi kwadoro echiche a, ebe Green Party kwere nkwa ịrụ ọrụ ụbọchị anọ n’izu n’ime oge ndọrọndọrọ ọchịchị 2017.
Labour Party anaghị akwado ebumnuche ahụ ugbu a dịka otu, kosiladị.
Onye nkwuchite okwu Labour Party kwuru: ‘Ọrụ ụbọchị anọ n’izu abughị amụma ndị otu a nke na ndị otu a anaghị atule ya.’
Shadow Chancellor John McDonnell jiri ọgbakọ Labour mere izu gara aga were kọwapụta echiche ya maka mgbanwe na akụnụba.
Mazị McDonnell kwuru na o kpebiri iweghachite ikike site na n’aka ndị ‘isi ụlọ ọrụ amaghị’ yana “ndị nrite oke uru’ n’ụlọ ọrụ ndị eji ebi ndụ.
Atụmatụ shadow chancellor ahụ pụtakwara na ndị nwere oke n’ụlọ ọrụ mmiri nwere ike ha agaghị enwetacha isi ego ha, maka gọọmentị Labour nwere ike ‘ime mwepu’ na ndabere ebumnobi ihe ezighi ezi.
O kwuputakwara atụmatụ itinye ndị ọrụ na bọdụ ụlọ ọrụ ma mepụta Inclusive Ownership Fund ga-enyefe pesenti 10 n’oke ụlọ ọrụ ndị nkịtị n’aka ndị ọrụ, ndị nwere ike inweta uru isi ego ruru £500.
Lindsey Graham, John Kennedy gwa “60 minutes” ma nyocha ndị FBI enwere ike ịgbanwe obi ha
Nyocha ndị FBI na-eme banyere ebubo eboro Ọka Ikpe Brett Kavanaugh egbuola oge ime ntuli aka ikpeazụ na nhọpụta ya maka Ụlọ Ikpe Kachasị Elu opekempe otu izu, wee bulite ajụjụ na nchọpụta ụlọ ọrụ ahụ enwere ike ịgbanwe obi ndị ọmebe iwu Repọblikan ịdọrọkwa nkwado ha.
N’ajụjụ ga-eme na Sọnde, onye akụkọ “60 Minutes” Scott Pelley jụrụ ndị Ọmebe Iwu Repọblikan John Kennedy na Lindsey Graham ma FBI enwere ike bọlite ihe ọ bụla ga-eme ka ha gbanwee obi ha.
Kennedy meghere onwe ya karịa onye otu ya si South Carolina.
“Ana m eche, ee,” Kennedy kwuru.
“E kwuru m na nbanye na nnụrịta ụka ahụ, E kwuru m, A gwara m Ọka Ikpe Kavanaugh okwu.
Akpọrọ m ya ka nke a mechara, ka ebubo ahụ pụtara, kwuo sị, ‘Ị mere ya?
Ọ kụjaghị, ọ nwere mkpebi, na enweghị mgbagha.”
Ntuli aka Graham, kosiladị, dịka edeela ya ede.
“Obi m ekpebiela gbasara Brett Kavanaugh, na ọ ga-ewe ebubo dasiri ike,” o kwuru.
“Dr. Ford, Amaghị m ihe mere mana a ama m nke a: Brett gọnarịrị nke ukwuu,” Graham gbakwunyere, na-arụta Christine Blasey Ford aka.
“Na ndị niile ọkpọrọ aha enweghị onye kwetara ya.
Ọ gbaala afọ 36.
Anaghị m ahụ ihe ọhụrụ na-agbanwe.”
Gịnị bụ Mmemme Global Citizen, na Ọ nwela Ihe Ọ Bụla Ọ Mere Iji Belata Ụbịam?
Satọde nke a New York ga-achịkọba Global Citizen Festival,emume ịgụ egwu a na-eme kwa afọ nke na-enwe ahịrị ndị ama ama na-atụ n’anya nke ukwuu na-eme ihe nkiri, yana ebumnobi dịkwa ịtụnanya; ịkwụsị ụbịam n’ụwa.
Ugbu a n’afọ nke asaa ya, Global Citizen Festival ga-ahụ puku kwụrụ puku mmadụ ga-ezute na Ama Central Park, nke abụghị naanị inweta ọṅụ n’ihe nkiri ndị a dịka Janet Jackson, Cardi B, Shawn Mendes, ma ka ha kwalitekwa mmata ezigbo ebumnuche mmemme ịkwụsị ụbịam na 2030.
Global Citizen Festival nke kwuputara na 2012, bụ alaka nke Global Poverty Project, otu nkwalite amụma mba ụwa nwere olile anya ịkwụsị ụbịam site na ịbawanye ọnụọgụ ndị na-alụso ya ọgụ.
Ka ị were nweta tịketị n’efu maka mmemme ahụ (beluso ma ọ masịrị gị ịkwụ ụgwọ tịketị), ndị ga-abịa ihe nkiri a ga-arụ ụfọdụ ọrụ, ma ọ bụ ‘mee ihe’ dịka nwepụta onwe n’ọrụ, izigara onye isi obodo ozi ịntanetị, ịkpọ oku ekwentị ma ọ bụ ụzọ ọ bụla bara uru iji were kpalite mmata ebumnuche ha ịkwụsị ụbịam.
Mana, kedu ka o si agara Global Citizen nke ọma ebe ha nwere naanị afọ 12 imejuputa ebumnuche ya?
Echiche inye ndị mmadụ tịketị n’efu, a bụ ụzọ ziri ezi iji kwanye ndị mmadụ ka ha kpọọ oku mmepụta ihe, ka ọ bụ naanị ụzọ ọzọ ihe akpọrọ “kliktivizm” - ndị chere na ha nwere ihe pụrụ iche ha na-eme n’ezie site na ibinye aka na mkpesa ịntanetị ma ọ bụ zipu tweet?
Kemgbe 2011, Global Citizen kwuru na ha enweela ”mmepụta ihe” nde 19 site n’aka ndị nkwado ya, na-akwa maka mmezu ebumnuche dị iche iche.
O kwuru na mmepụta ihe ndị a enyerela aka mee ndị na-achị achị na mba ụwa ka ha maa ọkwa nkwa yana amụma ruru ihe karịrị ijeri $37, nke ga-emetụta ndụ mmadụ karịrị ijeri 2.25 na 2030.
Na mbido 2018, otu ahụ rụtụrụ aka nkwa na ọkwa 390 nke malitere site na mmepụta ihe ya, opekempe ijeri $10 bụ nke ekesagoro ma ọ bụ tụta n’ego.
Otu ahụ na-ama amụma n’ego ndị echekwabara emetụtala n’ahụ mmadụ ruru nde 649 n’ụwa gbaa gburugburu.
Ụfọdụ nkwa ndị ekwere tinyere Power of Nutrition, mmekọrịta ndị ego nkwado dị na U.K yana ndị ntinye n’ọrụ wepụtara onwe ha “inyere ụmụaka aka itozu etozu ihe ha ga-abụ,” na-ekwe Rwanda nkwa nde $35 iji nyere ha aka kwụsị erighị nri na-edozi ahụ dị n’obodo ahụ ka ha nwetachara tweet karịrị 4,700 sitere na Global Citizen.
“Na nkwado sitere na gọọmentị UK, ndị na-enye onyinye na gọọmentị mba ọzọ, na Global Citizen dịka gị, anyị ga-eme mmeremme ezighi ezi nke erizughị nri na-edozi ahụ ka ọ bụrụ ozi mgbakwunye na hịstrị.” Onye nnọchi anya Power of Nutrition Tracey Ullman gwara igwe mmadụ n’oge emume egwu na London na Eprel 2018.
Otu ahụ kwukwara nke a ka emechara ihe mmepụta 5,000, na-akpọ U.K oku ka ha meziwanye nri ndozi ahụ maka ndị nne na ụmụaka, gọọmentị mara ọkwa inye ego maka ọrụ, Power of Nutrition, nke ga-eji enyemaka nri ndozi ahụ rute ụmụ-nwanyị na ụmụaka nde 5 aka.
N’azịza otu n’ime FAQ dị na ịntanetị ya, na-ajụ, “kedu ihe mere iji chee na anyị nwere ike ịkwụsị oke ụbịam?”
Global Citizen zara: “Ọ ga-abụ ụzọ tere aka ma sie ike - mgbe ụfọdụ anyị ga ada ma daa mba.
Mana, dị ka oke ndọrọndọrọ ikike dịịrị mmadụ yana mmegide ịkpa oke mere tupu anyị, anyị ga-emeri, n’ihi na anyị siri ike karịa ma ejikọọ ọnụ.
Janet Jackson,The Weeknd, Shawn Mendes, Cardi B, Janelle Monáe bụ otu n’ime ndị ga-eme ihe nkiri na mmemme nke afọ a na New York, bụ nke Deborra-Lee Furness na Hugh Jackman ga-achịkọba.
US nwere ike iji Ndị Agha Mmiri maka “mgbachi” were gbochie nbufe ahịa Ike ndị Russia- Ọde Akwụkwọ Obodo
Washington nwere ike “ma ọ dị mkpa” jiri Ndị Agha Mmiri ha nwere gbachie ike Russia ibanye ahịa, tinyere Middle East, Ọde Akwụkwọ US Ryan Zinke kwuputara, dịka arụtụrụ aka na Washington Examiner.
Zinke boro ebubo na itinye aka nke Russia na Syria - nke ama ama, bụ ebe ọ na-arụ ọrụ n’ihi akpọmoku nke gọọmentị ziri ezi - bụ ụzọ aghụghọ iji nyochaa ahịa ike ọhụrụ.
“Ekwenyere m n’ihe kpatara ha jiri nọrọ na Middle East bụ ka ha zụọ ahịa ike dị ka ha na-eme na ọwụwa anyanwụ Europe, mgbada Europe,” o kwuru nke a.
Ma, dabere na onye ọrụ ahụ, enwere ụzọ na ka-esi agba ya mgba.
“United States nwere ike, jiri Ndị Agha Mmiri anyị, hụ na okporo ụzọ mmiri anyị ghe oghe, ma ọ bụrụ na ọ dị mkpa, gbachie, iji hụ na ike ha abaghị ahịa.” o kwuru.
Zinke na-agwa ndị bịara emume ndị Consumer Energy Alliance chịkọbara, otu anaghị achọ uru nke dobere onwe ya dịka “olu ndị na-eri ike” na US.
Ọ gara tulee usoro Washington ji emeso Russia na Iran omume, chọpụta na ha abụọ bụ otu.
“Nhọrọ akụnụba Iran na Russia bụ, dabere naanị, ịgbazinye na iweghachi mmanụ ọkụ ụgbọ ala,” o kwuru, ebe ọ na-arụtụ Russia aka dị ka “ọgba otu egwu” nwere akụnụba dabere na mmanụ ọkụ na unyi ekereụwa.
Nkwuputa ndị a pụtara ka ọchịchị Trump na-agbalị ịkwalite ibufe ahịa mmiri gaasị ọnatarachi ha na Europe, ịnọchi Russia, bụ nke ka dị ọnụala maka ndị na-eri ahịa nke Europe.
Maka imezu nke a, ndị ọrụ ọchịchị Trump tinyere Onye Isi Ala US Donald Trump n’onwe ya, na-agbalị ịkwanye Germany ka ọ pụta na atụmatụ ọwa mmiri Nord Stream 2 “adịghị mma”, bụ nke dabere na Trump, mere Berlin “onye nke Moscow ji eji.
Moscow ekwuola ugboro ugboro na ijeri $11 ọwa mmiri Nord Stream 2 ahụ, bụ nke emebere ka o bulie ike ọwa mmiri nke dị adị ruo ijeri 110 kubik mita, bụ naanị atụmatụ maka akụnụba.
Kremlin na-arụ ụka na oke mgbachi nke Washington n’atụmatụ ahụ bụ naanị n’ihi akụnụba bụ ihe kpatara ya ma bụrụ ọmụmatụ asompi n’adịghị mma.
“Ekwenyere m na anyị na-ahụkọrịta na ike enweghị ike ịbụ ngwaọrụ eji eme nkwanye, ndị na-eri ahịa kwesịrị ịhọrọ onye mbunye ahịa ya,” Mịnịsta Ike nke Russia Aleksandr Novak kwuru, sotere nnọkọ ya na Ọde Akwụkwọ Ike nke US Rick Perry na Moscow na Septemba.
Ọnọdụ US ebutela nkwụtọ si Germany, bụ nke kwuputakwara nkwado ha n’atụmatụ ahụ.
Ụlọ ọrụ na-achị na Germany maka ụlọ nrụpụta ihe, Federation of German Industries (BDI), akpọkuola US ka ha wepu aka na amụma ike nke Europe yana nkwekọrịta obodo na obodo dị n’etiti Berlin na Moscow.
“Enwere m nnukwu nsogbu mgbe obodo nke atọ n’etinye anya na mbunye ahịa ike anyị,” Dieter Kempf onye isi Federation of German Industries (BDI) kwuru, sotere nnọkọ dị n’etiti German Chancellor Angela Merkel na Onye Isi Ala Vladmir Putin.
Elizabeth Warren “Ga-elebe Anya Nke Ukwuu” Na Ịzọ Maka Onye Isi Ala na 2020, Onye Ọmebe Iwu Massachusetts Kwuru
Onye ọmebe iwu Massachusettes Elizabeth Warren kwuru na Satọde na ya “ga-elebe anya nke ukwuu” ịzọ maka onye isi ala, sotere ntuli aka ọkara ọchịchị.
N’oge nzụkọ obodo na Holyoke, Massachusetts, Warren kwuputakwara na ya ga-atule ịzọ ọkwa.
“O ruola oge ụmụ-nwanyị ga-aga na Washington were jee dozie gọọmentị anyị mebiri emebi, bụ nke tinyere ụmụ-nwanyị ịnọ n’isi.” o kwuru, dabere na The Hill.
“Nọvemba 6 gachaa, A ga-elebe anya nke ukwuu n’ịzọ maka onye isi ala.”
Warren tinyere ọnụ na Onye Isi Ala Donald Trump n’ime oge nzụkọ obodo ahụ, na-ekwu na ọ “na-eduba obodo a n’ụzọ adịghị mma.
“Uche na-eche m ruo n’ọkpụkpụ banyere ihe Donald Trump na-eme ọchịchị onye kwuo uche ya nke anyị,” o kwuru.
Warren na-ekwuwapụta nkọcha ya maka Trump yana onye nhọpụta Ụlọ Ikpe Kachasị Elu ya, Brett Kavanaugh.
Na tweet Fraịde Warren kwuru ”n’ezie anyị chọrọ nyocha FBI tupu ntuli aka.”
Nyocha ewepụtara na Tọsde, kosiladị, gosiri ọtụtụ ndị okpuru ọchịchị ntuli aka nke Warren echeghị na ọ kwesịrị ịzọ ọkwa na 2020.
Pesentị Iri ise na asatọ nke “ndị nwere ike” ime ntuli aka nke Massachusetts kwuru na ọmebe iwu ahụ ekwesịghị ịzọ ọkwa, dabere na nyocha nke Suffolk University Poilitical Research Center/Boston Globe.
Pesentị Iri atọ na abụọ kwadoro yabụ ịzọ ọkwa.
Nyocha ahụ gosiri nkwado karịa maka ịzọ ọkwa nke Governor Deval Patrick chịburu ọchịchị, nke nwere pesentị 38 na-akwado ya ịzọ ọkwa ebe pesentị 48 megidere ya.
Aha ndị Demokrat ndị ukwuu ekwutere banyere ịzọ ọkwa nke 2020 tinyere Osote Onye Isi Ala Joe Biden chịburu ọchịchị na Onye Ọmebe iwu Vermont Bernie Sanders.
Biden kwuru na ya ga-eme mkpebi nke ya na Jenuarị, Associated Press kwuputara.

Anwudoro ya wee gbaa ya akwụkwọ maka ime ihe ike n’ụlọ n’abalị Mọnde
“Ihe nwa m nwoke na-agabiga, ihe ọ na-agabiga na nlaghachi azụ, Enwere m ike inwe nghọta ezinụlọ ndị ọzọ n’ahụ nsonazụ PTSD yana ụfọdụ ihe mmerụ ahụ ndị agha anyị na-eji alata,” ọ gwara ndị nọ na nnọkọ ndọrọndọrọ a maka Donald Trump na Tulsa, Oklahoma.
Palin kpọrọ nwudo ya ‘enyi nọ n’ime ụlọ” wee kwuo maka nwa ya nwoke na ndị ọzọ gara agha, ha na-alaghachi azụ dị obere iche, ha na-alaghachi azụ nwee obi ike, ha na-alaghachi na-ajụ ma enwere nsọpụrụ enwere maka ndị agha ibe ya, ndị agha ikuku, na ndị ọ bụla nọ n’otu ndị agha, n’ihe ha nyegoro obodo ha.”
Anwudoro ya na Mọnde na Wasilla, Alaska, wee gbaa ya akwụkwọ maka imeso nwanyị ihe ike n’ụlọ, mgbochi na mkpesa nke ime ihe ike n’ụlọ yana iji ngwa ọgụ ka oriri ihe na-egbu egbu, dabere na Dan Bennett, onye nkwuchite okwu ndị Wasilla Police Department.
Obodo 18, D.C na-akwado ịche aka mgba nke amụma mgbata ọsọ ndụ ọhụrụ
Obodo iri na asatọ yana District of Colombia na-akwado ịche aka mgba n’ụzọ iwu nke amụma U.S ọhụrụ nke anaghị enye nchekwa maka ndị na-agbata ọsọ ndụ n’ihi otu ndị ike ma ọ bụ ihe ike ime ụlọ.
Ndị nnọchi anya si obodo 18 ahụ na district gbara akwụkwọ ndị ọ metụtara inyere aka na Fraịde na Washington iji kwado onye mgbata ọsọ ndụ nke na-echere amụma ahụ aka mgba, NBC News kwuputara.
Ekwuputabeghị aha ndepụta n’uju nke onye na-agba akwụkwọ n’okwu Grace v. Sessions nke American Civil Liberties Union gbara na Ọgọst megide amụma etiti obodo.
O kwuru na onye ya na ya bi “na ndị otu ike ụmụ ya nwoke” megburu ya, ma ndị ọrụ U.S gbachibidoro arịrịọ ya maka mgbata ọsọ ndụ na Julaị 20.
Akpọchiri ya na Texas.
Ndị ọka iwu obodo nke na-akwado Grace kọwara na El Salvador, Honduras na Guatemala, mebere ọnụọgụ kacha na ndị na-etinye akwụkwọ maka mgbata ọsọ ndụ na U.S, dịka mba na-alụso ọgụ mbawanye otu ndị ike na ihe ike ime ụlọ.
Amụma ọhụrụ nke U.S megharịrị mkpebi 2014 nke Board of Immigrant Appeals mere na-anabata ndị mbịambịa ejighị akwụkwọ na-agba ọsọ ihe ike ime ụlọ itinye akwụkwọ mgbata ọsọ ndụ.
Onye Isi Ọka Iwu District of Columbia Karl Racine kwuru na nkwuputa Fraịde na amụma ọhụrụ ahụ “n’eleghara anya iwu nke obodo, etiti obodo na mba ofesi nke afọ kwụrụ afọ.”
“Iwu etiti obodo chọrọ na a ga-eme mkpebi na mkpesa ndị mgbata ọsọ ndụ ọ bụla n’ihe akaebe na ọnọdụ mkpesa ahụ, nke n’ụdị mgbachi ahụ na-emegide usoro iwu ahụ, “ịgba akwụkwọ ndị ọ metụtara inyere aka” kwuru.
Ndị ọka iwu gara n’ihu na-arụ ụka n’akwụkwọ ha gbara na amụma ahụ ịgbachi ndị mbịambịa ịbata na-emerụ akụnụba U.S ahụ, na-ekwu na ha na-abụkarị ndị nọrọ onwe ha azụ ahịa ma “na-enye ndị ọrụ ngo achọrọ.”
Onye Isi Ọka Iwu Jeff Sessions nyere ndị ọka ikpe iwu gbasara ndị mbịambịa, ka ha ghara inyezi nchekwa maka ndị mgbata ọsọ ndụ na-agbanarị mmegbu ihe ike ime ụlọ na otu ndị ike na Juun.
“Nchekwa mgbata ọsọ ndụ dịịrị ndị na-ahapụ obodo ha n’ihi mkpagbu ma ọ bụ ụjọ n’ihi agbụrụ, okpukpe, obodo onye si, ma ọ bụ nsonye n’otu mmekọrịta ọha ma ọ bụ echiche gbasara ndọrọndọrọ ọchịchị,” Sessions kwuru na ịma ọkwa amụma ya na Juun 11.
Emebeghị nchekwa mgbata ọsọ ndụ ka obeleta nsogbu niile enwere - ọbụlagodi nsogbu niile siri ike - nke ndị mmadụ n’ahụ n’ụwa niile.
Mbọ agwụ ike ịzọpụta ndị gbanarịrị ihe mberede na Palu dịka ọnụọgụ ndị nwụrụ anwụ na-agbago
Maka ndị gbanarịrị ihe mberede, ọnọdụ ahụ na-esiwanye ike.
“Ọ na-adị oke echiche,” Risa Kusuma kwuru, nne nke gbara afọ 35, na-agụgụ nwa nwoke ya na-amajiji n’ebe ndị gbapụrụ ọsọ n’obodo Palu mebiri emebi nọ.
“Nkeji ọ bụla ụgbọ ala ihe mberede na-ebute ozu.
Mmiri dị ọcha dị ụkọ.”
Ahụrụ ndị bi n’obodo ka ha na-alaghachi n’ụlọ ha mebiri emebi, na-atụta ihe n’arịa ndị mmiri juru, na-agbalị ịzọpụta ihe ndị ọ bụla ha nwere ike.
Narị kwụrụ narị mmadụ merụrụ ahụ na ụlọ ọgwụ nke ala ọmajiji ruru 7.5 mebiri, juputara.
Ụfọdụ ndị merụrụ ahụ tinyere Dwi Haris, onye nke azụ na ubu ya gbajiri, nọ n’ihu ilo Palu Army Hospital ezu ike, ebe a na-elete ndị merụrụ ahụ n’ilo n’ihi ọmajiji siri ike ka na-aga n’ihu.
Anya mmiri juru ya anya ka ọ na-akọ ka ajọ ala ọmajiji ahụ siri kwaa elu ụlọ nke ise ụlọ nkwari akụ ya na nwunye ya na nwa ya nwanyị nọ.

Echere m na afanyere m n’ime mgbawa dị n’ahụ aja, Harris gwara Associated Press, na-agbakwunye n’ezinụlọ ya batara n’obodo ịga agbamakwụkwọ.
